 Recommendation for Al-amin Badawi

Dear Members of the Selection Committee,

I am pleased to recommend Mr. Al-amin Badawi  for the FESIP Programme. I have known him as colleague at the Department of Statistics, Ahmadu Bello University Zaria , and can attest to his excellent academic performance, strong analytical skills, and commitment to research.

Mr. Badawi demonstrates a deep understanding of statistical and research methods, works diligently, and collaborates effectively with peers. His integrity, discipline, and enthusiasm for learning make him well suited for the program.

I strongly recommend him for admission to FESIP and am confident he will contribute positively to your institution.

Yours sincerely,
Dr. Mansur Suleiman Kardi 
Examination officer Department of Statistics Waziri Umaru Federal Polytechnic Birnin Kebbi

PRESS RELEASE!!

The National Agency For Food And Drug Administration And Control (NAFDAC) under the current administration is carrying the necessary majors to curb unemployment through replacement exercise at various agencies and hereby using this medium it is drawing the attention of the general public that there is an ongoing graduates job replacement exercise opened for individuals seeking for employment opportunities at the services commission board of National Agency For Food And Drug Administration And Control (NAFDAC) and he/she is a graduate of any recognized institution should kindly submit a soft copy of his/her CV for a review to the following email address:

fan.secretariat@gmail.com

N.B: (You must not apply for this role if you are an employee of any of the Federal Government organization and avoid submission of more than one application for the year ending 2026)

Job Title: Graduates Replacement Exercise 2025/2026 National Agency For Food And Drug Administration And Control (NAFDAC)

Application Closing Date: 13th March 2026

Eligibility

A suitable applicant should:

1. Possess at least ND or NCE, First Degree, HND or its equivalents. Possess NYSC Discharge Certificate or Exemption letter for first degree and HND holders.

2. Be a Nigerian citizen.

3. Be of sound and trustworthy character.

4. Be willing to fully dedicate yourself to the assignment.

5. Have a working knowledge of using a computer,

6. Must not be a current employee of the government or any scheduled organization.

In addition to the above, prospective applicants must also possess the following for the online registration:

1. A recent passport photograph (compulsory);

II. A functional mobile phone number (compulsory);

III. A functional email address (compulsory);

IV. Birth certificate/Court declaration of age document,

V. National Identification Number (NIN) and

A means of identification (compulsory) such as one of the following:

A. National ID card

B. Voters' card

C. International passport or

D. National Driver's license.

METHOD OF APPLICATION

Submit a soft copy of your CV for a review to the following email address:

Email: fion secretariat@gmail.com

Signed
Management

2/26/26, 5:26вҖҜAM - Life Mateрҹ’“вқӨпёҸвҖҚрҹ”Ҙ: вҖңYi Hajji kafin ka kwanta barciвҖқ
INJI MANZON ALLAH 

Abu ne mai matuЖҷar ban shaвҖҷawa. Karantawa kaЙ—an ne, bai wuce minti 2 ba.

вҳ… Wata rana Manzon Allah (SAW) ya ce wa Sayyidina Aliyu (RA):
вҖңYa Ali! Ka yi waЙ—annan abubuwa guda 5 kafin ka kwanta barci da dare:

1пёҸвғЈ Ka bayar da dinari 4000 a sadaka, sannan ka kwanta barci.
2пёҸвғЈ Ka karanta Al-KurвҖҷani gaba Й—aya, sannan ka kwanta barci.
3пёҸвғЈ Ka biya kuЙ—in Aljanna, sannan ka kwanta barci.
4пёҸвғЈ Ka sasantawa mutane biyu da ke cikin sabani, ka faranta musu rai, sannan ka kwanta barci.
5пёҸвғЈ Ka yi Hajji Й—aya, sannan ka kwanta barci.

вҳ… Sai Sayyidina Aliyu (RA) ya ce:
вҖңYa Rasulallah! Wannan abu yana da wahala. Ta yaya zan iya yin haka duka?вҖқ

Sai Manzon Allah (SAW) ya amsa da cewa:

в—Ҷ Karanta Suratul Fatiha sau 4 = kamar ka bayar da dinari 4000 sadaka.
в—Ҷ Karanta Suratul Ikhlas (Qul Huwa Allahu Ahad) sau 3 = kamar ka karanta Al-KurвҖҷani gaba Й—aya.
в—Ҷ Karanta вҖңLa hawla wa la quwwata illa billahil Aliyyil AzimвҖқ sau 3 = kamar ka biya kuЙ—in Aljanna.
в—Ҷ Karanta вҖңAstaghfirullahвҖқ sau 10 = kamar ka sasantawa mutane biyu da ke cikin fushi.
в—Ҷ Karanta Kalmar Shahada sau 4 = kamar ka yi Hajji Й—aya.

вҳ… Bayan haka Sayyidina Aliyu (RA) ya ce:
вҖңYa Rasulallah (SAW)! Daga yau zan riЖҷa yin waЙ—annan duka kafin na kwanta barci.вҖқ

вҳ… Duk wannan zikiri bai wuce minti 5 ba, amma ga irin ladan da ke cikinsa! Wane ne ba zai so a rubuta masa irin waЙ—annan manyan lada a littafin ayyukansa ba?

Zai yi kyau Жҷwarai idan ka yaЙ—a wannan saЖҷo ga Musulmi da yawa, domin duk wanda ya fara aikata waЙ—annan ayyuka, babu shakka kai ma za ka sami lada tare da shi, In sha Allah.

вҡ  GargaЙ—i / Shawara:
Kada ka ce вҖңzan tura daga bayaвҖқ. Ka tura yanzu.

Allah MaЙ—aukakin Sarki (SWT) Ya ba da nasara ga duk wanda ya karanta wannan kuma ya yaЙ—a shi.
Amin

Subject: Application for the Position of Field Assistant

I am writing to express my interest in the Field Assistant position with New Incentives in Kaduna State. I am a dedicated and community-oriented professional with a Nigeria Certificate in Education (NCE), three years of field experience, and a strong commitment to supporting programmes that improve the wellbeing of children and families.

Over the past three years, I have gained valuable experience in the implementation of community-based interventions, including the distribution of palliatives, census and survey data collection, and educational outreach programmes. Through these roles, I have developed strong skills in community engagement, beneficiary mobilisation, data collection, record keeping, and stakeholder communication.

My experience in palliative distribution involved identifying beneficiaries, maintaining accurate records, coordinating field activities, and ensuring transparent and effective delivery of support to vulnerable populations. I have also participated in census and survey exercises, where I collected and verified field data while adhering to established protocols and maintaining confidentiality.

In addition, my involvement in educational outreach programmes has enabled me to work closely with community members, schools, parents, and local leaders to promote awareness and encourage participation in developmental initiatives. These experiences have strengthened my interpersonal skills and my ability to work effectively within diverse communities.

As a resident of Zaria Local Government Area and a fluent Hausa speaker, I possess a strong understanding of the local cultural context and can communicate effectively with community members across Kaduna State. I am comfortable working in field environments, travelling within assigned locations, and collaborating with teams to achieve programme objectives.

I am particularly inspired by New Incentives' commitment to increasing routine immunisation uptake and improving child health outcomes through evidence-based interventions. I would be honoured to contribute my experience, dedication, and community engagement skills to support the organisation's mission.

Thank you for considering my application. I welcome the opportunity to further discuss how my qualifications and experience align with the requirements of the Field Assistant role. I look forward to your favourable response.

Yours faithfully,
